   <script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function(){
 	//console.log('===========');
     var productId = '#' + 122795;
     var revert = '\'revert\'';
     var zoomUrl = 'https://ii.chadwicks.com/fcgi-bin/iipsrv.fcgi?FIF=/images/chadwicks/source/products/110479_kha_alt1.tif&qlt=75&wid=220&cvt=jpeg';
    // console.log('zoomUrl  ' + zoomUrl);
     //console.log('productId  ' + productId);
     var url = zoomUrl;
 	$(productId).bind({
 		  mouseover: function(event) {
 		    var srcImg = $(productId).children(":first");
 		    //console.log('srcImg[0]  ' + srcImg[0]);
 		    //console.log('url  ' + url);
 		    if(srcImg[0] !== undefined && srcImg[0] !== '' && url !== undefined && url !== '' ){
 		    	addImagePath(srcImg[0], url);
 		    }
 		  },
 		  mouseleave: function(event) {
 		   var srcImg = $(productId).children(":first");
 		  // console.log('srcImg[0]  ' + srcImg[0]);
 		   //console.log('revert  ' + revert);
 		   
 		   if( url !== undefined && url !== ''){ 
 		    if(srcImg[0] !== undefined && srcImg[0] !=='' ){
 		   		removeImagePath(srcImg[0], revert);
 		  	 		}
 		  		}
 		  	}
 	});
 });
   </script>

   <script>
    var orig_url = null;
     function urlExists(img, newUrl, callback) {
         $(img).error(callback).attr('src', newUrl);
     }
     
     function addImagePath(obj, newUrl) {
 		if (obj.getAttribute('data-deferred-src') !== obj.src) {
 			return;
 		}
         var oldUrl = obj.src;
         orig_url = oldUrl; 
         var newUrl = newUrl;
         if(newUrl){
         if(newUrl.trim().length > 0){
             urlExists(obj, newUrl, function() {
                 $(this).unbind("error").attr("src", oldUrl);
             });
         }
     }
     }
         
     function removeImagePath(obj, url){
         var oldUrl = obj.src;
         var newUrl = orig_url;
         if(newUrl){       
         if(newUrl.trim().length > 0){
             urlExists(obj, newUrl, function() {
                 $(this).unbind("error").attr("src", oldUrl);
             });
         }
     }
     }
     
     function generateClickEventCall(baynote_pid, baynote_widget, baynote_slot,baynote_tracking) {	
 	    console.log(" Now calling the generate click event");	
 	    console.log("baynote_pid->> "+ baynote_pid+ "  baynote_widget->> "+ baynote_widget + "  baynote_slot->> "+ baynote_slot + "  baynote_tracking->> "+ baynote_tracking);
 	   
 	    generateClickEvent(baynote_pid, baynote_widget, baynote_slot,BNData);
 	  
 		return true;
 	}
   </script>
